<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ITEM 1.01.&#160; ENTRY INTO A MATERIAL DEFINITIVE AGREEMENT</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On December 27,2004, the Registrant entered into agreements with Axion
Solutions, Inc (&#147;Axion&#148;) for the software and licensing rights of an integrated
business sysem made by PeopleSoft, Inc. (&#147;PeopleSoft&#148;). Axion is a business
partner of PeopleSoft.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .5in .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ITEM
9.01.&#160; FINANCIAL STATEMENTS AND EXHIBITS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Exhibits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">99.1&#160;&#160; End User License Agreement</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">99.2&#160;&#160; Addendum to End User License Agreement</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">99.3&#160;&#160; Order Form Schedule</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">party
having the right to disclose it without an obligation of confidentiality to
Discloser.&#160;&#160; For purposes of this Section,
a disclosure of Confidential Information will not render the Confidential
Information &#147;generally known to the public&#148; when the (i) disclosure is enjoined
by Discloser, (ii) disclosure is the subject of a written settlement agreement
between Discloser and a third party resolving a dispute between Discloser and
such third party as to the alleged wrongful disclosure of the Confidential
Information, provided that such information remains confidential pursuant to
the terms of the settlement, or (iii) disclosing party is held liable to
Discloser&#160; for damages in an action
alleging wrongful disclosure or misappropriation of the Confidential
Information.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">10.4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b>Recipient may provide access to and use of the
Discloser&#146;s Confidential Information only to those third parties that have a
need to use and access the Confidential Information in the course of providing
services to Recipient concerning Licensee&#146;s use of the Software and have agreed
to non-disclosure obligations substantially similar to those contained
herein.&#160; Disclosure of Discloser&#146;s
Confidential Information by any such third party will be deemed a breach by
Recipient hereunder.&#160; To the extent
Recipient may be required to disclose Confidential Information in a legal
proceeding, Recipient may make such disclosure provided that Recipient notifies
Discloser of such requirement prior to disclosure and makes diligent efforts to
avoid and/or limit disclosure, and cooperates with Discloser in seeking a
protective order.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#147;Concurrent User&#148; </font></b>means a User with an assigned &#147;user id&#148; that has executed an application
contained in a Software either through a menu selection, fast path, or hidden
selection. A User will be counted as a Concurrent User until the User signs off

same Licensee System utilizing the same &#147;user id&#148; initiated from the same
workstation shall be counted as one Concurrent User. However, sessions
initiated by one &#147;user id&#148; on more than one workstation, or by more than one &#147;user
id&#148; on the same workstation, shall be counted as multiple Concurrent Users. The
total number of Concurrent Users simultaneously using the Licensed Products at
any time may not exceed the Concurrent Licensed Users. The SPC provided for
Deployment Server(s) (as defined in Article 1, Number 26) will reflect the
total number Licensed Users assigned to the Deployment Server(s) divided by .6
(Example: Licensees with 30 Concurrent Users will be able to deploy up to 50
client PC platforms under this provision).</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#147;Transmitted Copies</font></b>&#148; means this Agreement, including any Schedules and other ordering
documents which are (i) copied or reproduced and transmitted via photocopy,
facsimile or process that accurately transmits the original documents; and (ii)
accepted by PeopleSoft.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Updates</font></b>&#148; means those subsequent releases of the Software and
Documentation which are generally made available to licensees of the Software
which are similarly situated to Licensee, as part of Support Services at no
additional charge, other than the fees for Support Services, media and handling
charges.&#160; Updates shall not include any
releases, enhancements, functionality or products which Axion licenses separately
or charges for separate from Support Services.&#160;
The use of an Update may be subject to additional terms and Licensee may
be required to agree to such terms in writing prior to receiving an Update.&#160; Updates are delivered only if and when
available.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

undersigned represent and warrant that they are authorized as representatives

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
addendum amends the <b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">Axion End User License Agreement</font></u></b>,
(&#147;Agreement&#148;) dated December&nbsp;27, 2004, by and between <b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">AXION
SOLUTIONS, INC.</font></u></b> (&#147;AXION&#148; shall have the meaning set forth in
such Agreement) and <b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">EARL SCHEIB, INC.</font></u> </b>in consideration of their mutual
promises and subject to its Terms and Conditions as follows.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">The following will replace Section&nbsp;4.1 (Fees and Payment Terms):</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">First payment for the Products indicated on the
PeopleSoft Order Form Schedule&nbsp;dated December&nbsp;27, 2004 in the amount
of $97,956.00 is due and payable no later than December&nbsp;30, 2004.&#160; Balance of the payment (payment in full) for
the Products and applicable sales tax as indicated on the PeopleSoft Order Form
Schedule&nbsp;and its Exhibit B in the amount of $170,260.44 is due and payable
on January&nbsp;27, 2005.&#160; Annual Support
fee as indicated on the PeopleSoft Order Form Schedule&nbsp;dated December&nbsp;27,
2004 in the amount of $49,591.00 plus applicable sales tax of $4,091.26 is due
and payable no later than January&nbsp;27, 2005.&#160; Payments which are not received on the due
date shall bear interest at the lesser of eighteen
percent (18%) per annum or the maximum rate allowed under applicable law.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">The following will replace Section&nbsp;4.5 (Fees and Payment Terms):</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the term of the Agreement, the Licensee will
pay to Axion an annual support fee for the Software as defined on all
Schedule(s); Axion may change such support fee upon thirty (30) days prior
written notice, provided however, such change will not become effective with
respect to each Licensee until the next annual renewal of its Coverage
Period.&#160; In the event Licensee fails to
pay such support fee, Axion shall not be obligated to provide the Support
Services or the Software Updates until such time all past due fees are paid in
full.&#160; Axion Solutions will invoice 60
days prior to end of the Period of Coverage, which upon payment of invoice will
extend Support coverage for a one (1) year period.&#160; Axion Solution agrees, that for a period of
three (3) years from the date of this Agreement, it will not increase its list
prices for maintenance services over the greater of either six percent (6%) per
year or the national rate of inflation for the preceding twelve (12) month
period, as measured for the Consumer Price Index by the United States Bureau of
Labor Statistics.&#160; The agreement to
provide support services will automatically renew as each year. Licensee may
cancel the support services agreement by providing Axion written notice at
least sixty (60) days in advance of the renewal date.&#160; Failure to pay the support services by the
renewal date will result in cancellation of the agreement, and may result in
Licensee being required to pay additional fees to reinstate the support
services agreement.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Upon
execution of this Agreement, the previous Agreement dated November&nbsp;30,
2004 will be terminated.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">THIS ADDENDUM, INCLUDING THE AGREEMENT OF WHICH IT IS A PART,
IS A COMPLETE AND EXCLUSIVE STATEMENT OF THE AGREMENT BETWEEN THE PARTIES,
WHICH SUPERSEDES ALL PRIOR OR CONCURRENT PROPOSALS AND UNDERSTANDINGS, WHETHER
ORAL OR WRITTEN, AND ALL OTHER COMMUNICATIONS BETWEEN THE PARTIES RELATING TO
THE SUBJECT MATTER OF THIS ADDENDUM</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.&#160;
Notwithstanding anything to the contrary in the Agreement, in the event
of a conflict between the terms and conditions of this Addendum and those
contained within the Agreement, the terms and conditions of this Addendum shall
prevail.&#160; All other terms and conditions
remain unchanged and are ratified hereby.&#160;
THIS ADDENDUM SHALL NOT BE EFFECTIVE UNTIL EXECUTED BY CUTOMER AND
ACCEPTED AND EXECUTED BY AN AUTHORIZED REPRESENTATIVE OF AXION.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">By execution,
signer certifies that signer is authorized to accept and execute this agreement
on behalf of Axion and Customer.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the authorized
officers of the parties hereto have executed this Agreement as of the date
below.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT 99.3</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ATTACHMENT 1 </font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ORDER FORM SCHEDULE</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(ENTERPRISE PRICING) </font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Order Form Schedule (&quot;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Schedule</font></b>&quot;) is made as of December 27,
2004 (&quot;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Schedule Effective Date</font></b>&quot;)
by and between Earl Scheib, Inc., with principal place of business at 15206
Ventura Boulevard, Suite 200, Sherman Oaks, CA 91403 (&quot;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Licensee</font></b>&quot;) and Axion Solutions, Inc.
(&quot;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Sublicensor</font></b>&#148;). This
Schedule shall be submitted to PeopleSoft USA after execution by both Licensee
and Sublicensor. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.5</font></b><b><font size="1" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:8.5pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Incremental
License Fees for the Reported Revenues (RR) Software. </font></b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Licensee
may use the RR Software licensed pursuant to this Schedule in accordance with
the terms of this Schedule and the Agreement, to process its data at no
additional license fee, provided that the Reported Revenues do not exceed
$100,000,000 (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Base Revenues</font></b>&#148;).
Each year ninety (90) days prior to the Anniversary Date, Licensee shall report
to Sublicensor the Reported Revenues as of such date, and, in the event the
Reported Revenues as of such date exceed the Base Revenues, Licensee shall pay,
on or before the applicable Anniversary Date, additional non-refundable,
non-cancelable license fees. Upon receipt of such license fees in the amount of
$24778, Licensee&#146;s Base Revenues shall be modified to increase by
$10,000,000.00 .&#160; Licensee shall pay as
many increments of $24778 as necessary so that the Base Revenues exceed the
Reported Revenues as of that particular Anniversary Date.&#160; &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Reported
Revenues</font></b>&#148; shall mean the gross revenues reflected in an audited
statement from its external accounting firm.&#160;
&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">RR Software</font></b>&#148; shall mean
those Software modules licensed pursuant to this Schedule which are priced
based upon Reported Revenues, as indicated in the Software/Services table in
the Exhibit(s) to this Schedule.</font></p>

otherwise set forth herein, capitalized terms used herein shall have the same
meaning ascribed to them in the EULA.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#147;Accessory Products&#148; </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">mean third party software delivered with
the Software as a convenience to Licensee, but not licensed under this
Agreement.&#160; They are licensed to Licensee
pursuant to individual end user license agreements that are contained in the
software. Accessory Products are not Supportable Modules.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Base Metric</font></b>&#148;
means that Metric limit for which Licensee and related entities are licensed to
use or benefit from the use of the Software.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Initial
Services Term</font></b>&#148; means the period beginning on the Schedule Effective
Date and terminating one (1) year thereafter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Metric</font></b>&#148;
means that size measurement utilized to: (i) measure the size of Licensee and
related entities licensed to use or benefit from the use of the Software; and
(ii) define the limitations of the license granted pursuant to the Agreement;
and includes Employee Count, Reported Revenues, Student Count, Customer Count
and Funds Raised .</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Support Services</font></b>&#148; means that particular
package of services as may be offered by Sublicensor and selected by Licensee
and which are designed to support the Supportable Modules, and the standard
terms and conditions thereto, in effect on the later of the following:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i) the date fees are received for such services
offered by Sublicensor which are designed to support the Supportable Modules,
and (ii) the first date of the period for which services offered by Sublicensor
which are designed to support the Supportable Modules are provided.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Supportable Modules</font></b>&#148; are those Software modules
for which Sublicensor and PeopleSoft offers some sort of maintenance services,
and are comprised of: (i) Software excluding the Third Party Software modules;
(ii) Tools; and (iii) those Third Party Software modules specifically
designated in the Schedule as &#147;Supportable Modules&#148;.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#147;Third Party Software</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#148; means that portion of the Software

Protection Procedures&#148;).&#160; The Software
Protection Procedures will not destroy any of Licensee&#146;s data or software.&#160; Licensee shall not circumvent or render
inoperative the Software Protection Procedures.&#160;
Licensee must notify PeopleSoft in writing fifteen (15) days prior to
any change in the type of hardware model.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;

either the Technology Foundation Software module or the Technology Foundation
Upgrade Software module in order to license any of the EnterpriseOne Application
Software Modules.</font></b></p>

shall be based on Employee Count.&#160;&#160; </font></p>

  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.64%;">
  <p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.34%;">

  </td>
  <td width="13%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:13.96%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">247,775.00</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="0%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:.54%;">

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(13) Unless otherwise explicitly indicated in this Exhibit, incremental
license fees for the EnterpriseOne Supply Chain Management Software modules
shall be based on either Reported Revenues or, if Licensee is a PeopleSoft
Education and Government customer, on Reported Budget.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(14) Licensee must have a license for Manufacturing &#150; Shop Floor,
Manufacturing &#150; PDM and Inventory Management.</font></p>

Inventory Management.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(16) Licensee must have a license for Manufacturing &#150; PDM and Inventory
Management.&#160; </font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(17) Licensee must have a license for Inventory Management.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.5</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Addendum to</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Order Form Schedule</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This addendum amends the <u>Order Form Schedule</u>, (&#147;Schedule&#148;) dated
December&nbsp;27, 2004, by and between <b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">AXION
SOLUTIONS, INC.</font></u></b>  <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">(&#147;Axion&#148;) </font></b>and
<b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">EARL SCHEIB, INC.</font></u> (&#147;Licensee&#148;) </b>in
consideration of their mutual promises and subject to its Terms and Conditions
as follows.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7. Customer Assurance Program.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.1 </font></b>PeopleSoft
or the Acquiring Entity (defined below) agrees to pay to Licensee: (a) the
Total Fees set forth in the table in this Schedule&nbsp;and paid to Axion,
minus any fees included on the Schedule&nbsp;for installation or consulting, (&#147;Payment&#148;)
if:</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)
on or before two (2) years from the Schedule&nbsp;Effective Date, PeopleSoft,
Inc. is Acquired (hereinafter, the &#147;Acquisition&#148;); and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)
on or before four (4) years from the Schedule&nbsp;Effective Date, the entity
that results from an Acquisition (&#147;Acquiring Entity&#148;):</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)
discontinues or materially reduces Support Services for the Supportable
Module(s) before the end of the Applicable Support Term, or</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)
declines to license to Licensee on a commercially reasonable basis PeopleSoft
Software Modules, or</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)
discontinues providing Updates for the Supportable Module(s); and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)
Licensee requests the Payment in writing from PeopleSoft or the Acquiring
Entity on or before the date that is fifty-one (51) months after the Schedule&nbsp;Effective
Date, and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)
Licensee is at the time the Payment is requested, and has been, a continuous,
compliant subscriber to Support Services and no monies are owed under its
agreements with Axion as of the date Payment is requested.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.2 </font></b>Notwithstanding
the foregoing, either PeopleSoft or an Acquiring Entity may:</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)
discontinue licensing one or more PeopleSoft Software Modules if such software
module does not operate substantially as warranted, or if third party
technology required for the operation or use of such software module is no
longer commercially available, and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)
discontinue providing Updates to Supportable Modules if:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a.
it may discontinue licensing the Supportable Module pursuant to Section&nbsp;7.2(i),
or</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">b.
Updates for such Supportable Module are not being provided by PeopleSoft as of
the date of the Acquisition.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
no event does this relieve PeopleSoft or an Acquiring Entity from providing
Support Services for the Supportable Module(s) licensed on this Schedule&nbsp;for
the duration of the Applicable Support Term.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.3 </font></b>The
Payment described in this Section&nbsp;is Licensee&#146;s sole and exclusive remedy
for any liability of PeopleSoft or its affiliates or the Acquiring Entity
arising out of or related to the events described in 7.1 (i) and (ii) above and
will be reduced by any other amounts or damages Licensee seeks or recovers from
PeopleSoft or the Acquiring Entity in relation to this Schedule&nbsp;or the
events described in 7.1</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)
and (ii) above.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.4 </font></b>This
Section&nbsp;will be effective only if this Schedule&nbsp;is executed by both
parties on or before the earlier of the following dates:</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)
the expiration date defined in this Schedule; (ii) the expiration or withdrawal
of the Oracle tender offer, or (iii) December&nbsp;31, 2004. If the Schedule&nbsp;is
not executed by such date, the offer set forth in this term is rescinded, all
terms are null and void, and neither party shall have any obligation in
relation thereto.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.5 </font></b>For
purposes of this Section&nbsp;only, the following terms are defined as set
forth below.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)
&#147;Acquired&#148; means:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)
Oracle Corporation or any &#147;affiliate&#148; (as defined in Rule 405 promulgated under
the Securities Act of 1933, as amended) of Oracle Corporation (Oracle
Corporation and such affiliates, collectively or individually, &#147;Oracle&#148;)
becomes the &#147;beneficial owner&#148; (as defined in Rule 13d-3 under the Securities
Exchange Act of 1934, as amended), directly or indirectly, of securities of
PeopleSoft, Inc. representing fifty-one percent (51%) or more of the total voting
power represented by PeopleSoft&#146;s then outstanding voting securities, or</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)
The consummation of a merger or consolidation of PeopleSoft, Inc. with Oracle,
other than a merger or consolidation which would result in the voting
securities of PeopleSoft, Inc. outstanding immediately prior thereto continuing
to represent (either by remaining outstanding or by being converted into voting
securities of the surviving entity) at least fifty-five percent (55%) of the
total voting power represented by the voting securities of PeopleSoft, Inc. or
such surviving entity outstanding immediately after such merger or consolidation,
or</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)
The consummation of the sale or disposition by PeopleSoft, Inc. of all or
substantially all of PeopleSoft, Inc.&#146;s assets to Oracle.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)
&#147;Applicable Support Term&#148; means the period that PeopleSoft offers to provide
Support Services (generally four (4) years) for the Supportable Modules.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)
&#147;PeopleSoft Software Modules&#148; means all PeopleSoft software modules available
for licensing as of the</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">date
of the Acquisition.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)
&#147;Supportable Module(s)&#148; means the module(s) developed by PeopleSoft using its
underlying application development platform PeopleTools, which is licensed on
this Schedule&nbsp;for the database(s) indicated on the Schedule.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(v)
&#147;Support Services&#148; means the package of services offered by PeopleSoft and paid
for by Licensee and which are designed to support the Supportable Modules, and
the standard terms and conditions thereto, in effect as of the Schedule&nbsp;Effective
Date.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(vi)
&#147;Updates&#148; means subsequent releases of the Software and Documentation which are
a) generally made available as part of Support Services to licensees of the
Supportable Modules running on the same database platform, operating system and
hardware as Licensee for no additional license fee, and b) substantially
similar in frequency and quality when compared overall to the frequency and
quality of updates (i) that Acquiring Entity delivers to licensees of its
products that are substantially similar in function and purpose to the
Supportable Modules (&#147;Acquiring Entity Modules&#148;) or (ii) if there are no
Acquiring Entity Modules, that PeopleSoft delivered for the Supportable Modules
in the most recent major release cycle completed prior to the Acquisition.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.6 </font></b>For
any term defined in this Section, such definition shall be the sole definition
for purposes of interpreting this Section. In construing this Section&nbsp;only,
if there is any conflict between the terms of this Section&nbsp;and any other
term, the terms of this Section&nbsp;shall control.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
undersigned represent and warrant that they are authorized as representatives
of the party on whose behalf they are signing to sign this Software License and
Services Agreement and to bind their respective party thereto.</font></p>
